msg:I donâ€™t know how many people were fooled by the reviews. In fact, it is not as perfect as they say. I booked an executive room. As soon as I entered the room, there was a smell of cigarette smoke mixed with damp musty smell. I thought about turning on the air freshener to circulate it, but when I turned on the machine, dust and a small insect were blown out. The curtains were also broken and the buttons were malfunctioning. Able to pull by hand. The executive room is large, but the TV is very small and the sound is also low. No one can talk in the room with the TV on, otherwise the TV sound will not be heard. The blinds in the bathroom are not closed tightly, so you can watch others using the toilet in the room. Sound insulation is not good either. The service was not as good as the reviews said. When I checked in, I was asked if I drove a car. I said I drove a car, and then nothing happened. When I checked out, the front desk asked me if the license plate number was not recorded when I checked in? What kind of work connection is this? ! There is no wine in the executive lounge, no service staff, only Sprite, Fanta and several types of tea. The kettle is not connected to the power supply, only cold water, and the lounge is only open in the afternoon. Is this called an executive lounge? No wonder many people commented on the free upgrade to an executive room because there is no generally accepted executive trea**ent.
